<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 2.02&#160; Results of Operations and Financial
Condition.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On&#160; January 26, 2005, the Registrant issued a
press release and held a conference call with analysts to report on the results
of operations for the fiscal year 2004, which ended on November 30, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Furnished with this Form
8-K as Exhibit 99.1 is a copy of the press release labeled &#147;McCormick Reports
Record Results For Fourth Quarter And Fiscal Year,&#148; which includes a
Consolidated Income Statement for the three and twelve month periods ended
November 30, 2004 and November 30, 2003, a Consolidated Balance Sheet of the
Registrant as of November 30, 2004 and November 30, 2003, and an Consolidated
Statement of Cash Flows for the twelve months ended November 30, 2004 and
November 30, 2003.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

Statements and Exhibits</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&#160; Exhibits</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The exhibits to this
report are listed in Item 2.02 above and in the Exhibit Index that follows the
signature line.</font></p>

  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>

<body lang="EN-US" link="blue" vlink="purple">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE
RELEASE</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">McCORMICK</font></u></b><b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;"> REPORTS RECORD RESULTS FOR<br>
FOURTH QUARTER AND FISCAL YEAR</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SPARKS, MD, JANUARY 26&nbsp;&nbsp;-&nbsp;&nbsp;-&nbsp;&nbsp;-&nbsp;&nbsp;McCormick
&amp; Company, Incorporated (NYSE:MKC), today
reported record sales and earnings per share from continuing operations for the
fiscal year ended November 30, 2004:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Sales increased 11%, reaching $2.5 billion</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Operating income increased 13%</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Net cash from continuing operations rose to $349
million compared to $202 million in 2003</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Dividends paid rose 20%</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Record fiscal year results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the fiscal year,
McCormick reported a record $2.5 billion in sales, an increase of 11% above
2003.&#160; This sales growth was achieved
with a 4% increase in volume, 4% from favorable foreign exchange rates, a 2%
benefit from acquisitions, and a 1% increase in pricing and product mix.&#160; Higher volumes were achieved with new
products, expanded distribution and more effective marketing.&#160; In 2004, new products developed in the past
three years comprised 13% of sales.&#160; The
Company acquired Zatarain&#146;s in June 2003 and
benefited from incremental sales in the first half of 2004.&#160; In November 2004, the Company acquired Silvo, which is expected to generate $50 million of sales
in 2005.&#160; This business added&#160; $4 million to sales in the fourth quarter of
2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In addition to the sales
growth achieved in 2004, gross profit reached $1.0 billion.&#160; Gross profit margin increased 0.3 percentage
points to 39.9%.&#160; Cost reductions and a
shift to more value-added products improved gross profit margin.&#160; These improvements were partially offset by
higher costs of employee benefits, insurance, fuel and other expenses.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At the beginning of 2004,
a three-year goal was set to reduce costs by $70 million, with $15 million
projected for the first year.&#160; The
Company exceeded this projection and generated $24 million in cost savings
during 2004, with reductions in both cost of goods sold and operating
expenses.&#160; The Company continues to
project cost reductions of $25 million in 2005 and $30 million in 2006.&#160; In 2004, the cost reductions as well as
proceeds from a lawsuit settlement were invested in initiatives to grow sales
and profits.&#160; These included higher
advertising and research and development costs, which increased 43% and 18%
respectively, in 2004.&#160; In addition, a
program to reorganize international operations was initiated during 2004.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\rsampat\05-2252-1\task282326\2252-1-mm.htm',USER='rsampath',CD='Jan 26 09:47 2005' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2004, special credits
were $2 million, which was the net amount of $8 million from the lawsuit
settlement and $6 million of special charges that related to a streamlining action
program adopted at the end of 2001.&#160; In
2003, special charges of $5 million related to the 2001 streamlining action
program.&#160; With higher sales and improved
gross profit margin, operating income rose $37 million in 2004, an increase of
13%.&#160; Other income was $2 million in 2004
and $13 million in 2003.&#160; In 2003, the
Company recorded as other income a $5 million gain on the sale of an interest
in non-strategic royalty agreements and $5 million of interest income on the
purchase price refund from the acquisition of Ducros.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2004, net income from
continuing operations rose 8% to $215 million.&#160;
Earnings per share from continuing operations rose 9% to $1.52, an
increase of 12&#162; compared to 2003.&#160; The
primary factors driving this increase were higher sales and operating margin
that added 18&#162;.&#160; This was offset in part
by the decrease in other income of 5&#162;.&#160;
Other factors affecting earnings per share had a net negative impact of
1&#162;.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the 12 months ended
November 30, 2004, the net cash flow from continuing operating activities was
$349 million compared to $202 million for the prior year.&#160; Contributing to this increase was a $34
million reduction in inventory versus a $50 million increase in inventory
during 2003.&#160; Other factors included the
change in other assets and liabilities, a continued decrease in prepaid
allowances and higher net income from continuing operations.&#160; During 2004, McCormick used this cash and the
proceeds of stock option exercises to fund $174 million of share repurchases,
$77 million of dividends, the acquisition of Silvo
for $74 million and net capital expenditures of $67 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Record
fourth quarter results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales in the fourth
quarter of 2004 rose 7% to $744 million.&#160;
Sales volume increased 4%, and favorable foreign exchange rates contributed
3%.&#160; Consumer business sales were
particularly strong in the Americas, and Europe benefited from the acquisition
of Silvo.&#160;
Industrial sales benefited from new product activity offset in part by
initiatives to discontinue certain lower-margin products.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2004, gross profit
margin was 42.4% in the fourth quarter compared to 43.3% in the prior
year.&#160; During the fourth quarter, the
Company identified and corrected the operational accounting in an industrial
plant in Scotland.&#160; This adjustment related
to prior quarters and increased cost of goods sold by $6 million.&#160; The adjustment reduced gross profit margin by
0.9 percentage points in the fourth quarter.&#160;
Gross profit margin was also affected by higher costs of fuel, employee
benefits and other costs, partially offset by stronger consumer sales and the
benefit of cost reductions.&#160;&#160; Selling,
general and administrative costs as a percentage of sales were lower in the
fourth quarter of 2004, despite a 25% increase in advertising expense and a 19%
increase in research and development costs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings per share from
continuing operations were 62&#162; compared to 61&#162; in the fourth quarter of
2003.&#160; Operating income added 3&#162; to
earnings per share.&#160; This increase
included the impact of a 3&#162; decrease that was due to the operational accounting
adjustment.&#160;&#160; Earnings per share were 3&#162;
higher in 2003 because of the gain </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">on the sale of an
interest in non-strategic royalty agreements that was recorded in that
period.&#160; Other factors had a positive net
effect of 1&#162; and included fewer shares outstanding and a lower tax rate.&#160; Special charges were 2&#162; in the fourth quarter
in both 2004 and 2003.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Chairman&#146;s
Comments</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Robert J. Lawless,
Chairman, President &amp; CEO, commented, &#147;During 2004 we generated a
significant amount of cash and used this cash to build shareholder value in a
number of ways.&#160; Specifically, cash from
operations rose to $349 million, an increase of nearly $150 million compared to
2003.&#160; A significant portion of this
cash, $174 million, was used to repurchase shares during 2004.&#160; In addition, dividends paid to shareholders
were $77 million, an increase of 20% compared to 2003 and more than 30%
compared to 2002.&#160; With the acquisition
of Silvo for $74 million, we gained a leading
position in the spices and seasonings market in the Netherlands and in
Belgium.&#160; We also invested $67 million of
cash in software, equipment and facilities to support our operations and
advance our supply chain initiatives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;During 2004 we invested
in advertising and product development to grow sales.&#160; We also drove sales with more effective trade
promotions and distribution gains.&#160;
Excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange and the impact of
acquisitions, we increased sales 5%.&#160; Our
ongoing success in introducing value-added, consumer-preferred products is
evidenced by the shift in our sales.&#160; In
2004, we exceeded 70% as the portion of sales that are value-added products
versus spices, herbs and other ingredients.&#160;
In our consumer business we increased worldwide sales of grinders 36%
and of grilling products 8%.&#160; In our
industrial business we had particular success with coating systems and in the
U.S. achieved an increase of more than 30%.&#160;
Across both businesses, 13% of 2004 sales were from new products
developed in the past three years.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We completed our B2K
program in the U.S., and progress is being made toward&#160; an implementation in Europe and Canada.&#160; Supply chain initiatives achieved $24 million
of cost savings during 2004, a great start toward our three-year $70 million goal.
We also had some early success in reducing&#160;
&#147;SKU&#146;s&#148; (the number of different items sold) in the U.S. and in
Europe.&#160; We increased the productivity in
developing new products by more than 25% in 2004 as measured by sales per
research and development professional.&#160;
In China, we streamlined our business to 75 well-qualified distributors
from 250 in 2003.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;As a result of these
initiatives, investments and momentum, we are well-positioned for growth in
2005.&#160; We expect sales to grow in a 4-7%
range including an incremental $46 million from the acquisition of Silvo.&#160; Earnings per
share for 2005 is expected to range from $1.70-$1.74.&#160; This includes an estimated 1&#162; of special
charges as we conclude the streamlining actions announced at the end of
2001.&#160;&#160; Based on our current outlook for
the year, we expect to achieve a significant portion of the earnings per share
increase in the second half of 2005.&#160;
Both the sales and earnings per share goals for 2005 are in line with our
long-term annual objectives, which are to grow sales 3-7% and earnings per
share 10-12%.&#160; During the next three
years, we expect to generate approximately $450 million in cash from
operations, less dividends and net capital expenditures.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\rsampat\05-2252-1\task282326\2252-1-mm.htm',USER='rsampath',CD='Jan 26 09:47 2005' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;In summary, we are
pleased with our financial performance and business achievements of 2004.&#160; We have created strong momentum in product
development, marketing efforts and margin improvement initiatives as we look
ahead to 2005.&#160; It is the employees of
McCormick who are making our goals a reality and building value for the Company&#146;s
shareholders.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Business
Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the fiscal year,
sales for McCormick&#146;s consumer business rose 15% when compared to 2003.&#160; Higher volume added 10% to sales, of which 4%
was due to the incremental impact of the Zatarain&#146;s business
on the first half of the year.&#160; Favorable
foreign exchange added 4%, and positive price and product mix added 1%.&#160; In the Americas, sales increased 16% with 14%
from higher volume.&#160; New products, more
effective marketing and distribution gains drove an 8% volume increase, with
the remaining 6% attributable to the incremental impact of the Zatarain&#146;s acquisition on the first half of 2004.&#160; Consumer sales in Europe increased 14% in
2004, with 12% due to foreign exchange and 1% from the acquisition of Silvo.&#160; Under more
intense competitive conditions, the Company was able to hold sales volumes
about even with 2003.&#160; In the
Asia/Pacific region, consumer sales increased 11%, with most of the increase
due to favorable foreign exchange.&#160;&#160; In
China, sales growth was tempered by the Company&#146;s elimination of certain lower
margin items.&#160; Operating income from
continuing operations for the consumer business rose 17% to $270 million for
fiscal year 2004, despite a $15 million increase in advertising.&#160; This higher income was driven by strong sales
performance and cost reduction efforts.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the fourth quarter,
sales for McCormick&#146;s consumer business rose 8% when compared to 2003.&#160; Higher volume added 5% to sales, and
favorable foreign exchange added 3%.&#160; In
the Americas, sales increased 6% primarily as a result of higher volumes from
new products and more effective marketing.&#160;
Consumer sales in Europe increased 16% for the quarter, with 10% due to
favorable foreign exchange and 5% from the acquisition of Silvo
early in November.&#160; The Company was able
to achieve a 1% increase in sales volume, price and product mix during a period
of more intense competition, particularly in France.&#160; In the Asia/Pacific region, consumer sales
increased 10%, with 5% added by favorable foreign exchange and 5% due to an
increase in volume, price and product mix.&#160;
Operating income from continuing operations for the consumer business
rose 8% to $118 million for the fourth quarter of 2004, despite a $2 million
increase in advertising.&#160; This higher
income was driven by strong sales performance and cost reduction efforts.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the fiscal year,
sales for McCormick&#146;s industrial business increased 7% when compared to
2003.&#160; Higher volumes added 3%, favorable
foreign exchange added 3% and price and product mix added 1%.&#160; In the Americas, industrial sales rose 6%
primarily due to a 4% volume increase that was driven largely by new
products.&#160; Industrial sales in Europe
increased 12% as a result of favorable foreign exchange. A continued shift in
emphasis to higher margin products resulted in reduced sales of certain lower
margin products, offset by more favorable price and product mix during
2004.&#160; In the Asia/Pacific region,
industrial sales rose 9%, with a 6% contribution from favorable foreign
exchange and 3% from volume, price and product mix.&#160; Operating income for the industrial business
rose 4% to $114 million in 2004 and included a $6 million increase in research
and development costs.&#160;&#160; This increase in
income was the result of higher sales, an emphasis on more value-added,
higher-margin products and cost reduction efforts offset by the higher cost of
employee benefits, fuel and other expenses.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the fourth quarter of
2004, sales for McCormick&#146;s industrial business increased 4% when compared to
2003.&#160; Favorable foreign exchange added
2%, and higher volumes added 2%.&#160; In the
Americas, industrial sales rose 4% due to a 5% volume increase that was driven
largely by new products.&#160; Industrial
sales in Europe increased 4% for the quarter, with foreign exchange
contributing 9%. Sales decreased 5% due to the continued shift in emphasis to
higher margin products that reduced sales of certain lower margin
products.&#160; In the Asia/Pacific region,
industrial sales rose 8% in the fourth quarter, with 3% due to favorable
foreign exchange and 5% due to volume, price and product mix.&#160; Operating income for the industrial business
was $28 million for the fourth quarter of 2004, a decline of $1 million
compared to the prior year.&#160; The
operational accounting adjustment decreased operating income $6 million in the
fourth quarter.&#160; Increased sales and the
impact of cost reductions increased operating income $5 million.&#160; This increase was net of a $2 million
increase in research and development costs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Live Webcast</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As previously announced,
McCormick will hold a conference call with the analysts today at 11:00 a.m.
ET.&#160; The conference call will be web cast
live via the McCormick corporate web site http://www.mccormick.com.&#160; Click on &#147;Company Information&#148; then &#147;Investor
Services,&#148; and follow directions to listen to the call.&#160; At this same location, a replay of the call
will be available for one week following the live call.&#160; Past press releases and additional
information can be found at the Company&#146;s website.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
